          <div style="clear:right">
          </div>
          <div class="t withAv">
           It derives from a thought experiment often seen on 4chan.
           <br/>
           <br/>
           Basically you tell people to quickly think of three things that aren't Jackie Chan. A ludicrously simple task, but despite this, while thinking of three things you can't help but also think of Jackie Chan, violating the rules. It shows that the brain can not effectively understand negatives. The brain an be told to think of something, but it can't be told to not think of something.
           <br/>
           <br/>
           Why Jackie Chan? Why not?
          </div>
         </div>
        </div>
